static thread_local uint64_t results[size];
	for (int i = 0; i < size; i++) {
		results[i] = input ^ weights[i];
	}
	using sumover = uint8_t;
	constexpr int sumbits = sizeof(sumover) * 4;
	constexpr int finalbits = ((sizeof(uint64_t) / sizeof(sumover)) * BNN::size) / 4;

	sumover* vals = (sumover*)results;
	uint64_t target = 0;

	for (int i = 0; i < (sizeof(uint64_t) / sizeof(sumover)) * BNN::size; i++)
	{
		if (bitcount(vals[i]) < sumbits) {
			target |= (1ull << i);
		}
	}
return std::popcount(target) > finalbits; //> 16 of 64 bits set
